!learn add gourmand Amulet of the gourmand lets you eat chunks at any satiation level. However, it takes about 200 turns after wearing to fully kick in. The longer it's been on, the more nutrition you gain from chunks (linearly) and the less likely contaminated chunks are to make you nauseous. Saprovores with gourmand tread all chunks as rotten instead.
!learn add gourmand If you see 'tastes great' when eating a chunk, your amulet of the gourmand is fully charged. If you see 'is not very appetising', you only just put it on.

Higher card power level makes more of them available, and starts you higher up the list.

!learn add scroll_of_fog[1] For the "oh shit there's an oklob plant/pack of yaktaurs/etc and the nearest cover is 5 squares away" moments. Creates 8-15 tiles of fog centered on you - may be black smoke (25%) which spreads further on successive turns. 2 tiles of fog will block LOS mutually. This is a very valuable emergency-prevention scroll!
!learn del smoke
!learn add smoke Two tiles of smog in a row will block LOS mutually (like trees).
!learn edit smoke s/smog/smoke
!learn edit smoke s/$/ Certain kinds of smoke (like black smoke) spread to adjacent tiles, others just stay put.
!learn edit smoke s/in a row/on the same line
!learn add smoke Ways to get lots of smoke: Abjure a lot of summons at once (lasts one turn only), shoot a fire ammo/spell/breath weapon over water (or get it shot at you), read a scroll of fog, hang out in the abyss/swamp, get a smoke demon/steam dragon? to breathe at you...
!learn edit cloud s/and occasionally bugginess/primal chaos, and occasionally bugginess.
!learn edit cloud s/and occasionally bugginess/primal chaos, and occasionally bugginess
!learn edit cloud s/and occasionally bugginess/primal chaos and occasionally bugginess

!learn add kraken A powerful sea monster found in the {Shoals}. It keeps its main body out of reach and uses powerful tentacles (represented as seperate monsters with special AI) to attack you. The tentacles will advance when you are inside the main body's LoS, and retreat when you are outside it. Killing its tentacles hurts the kraken.
!learn add kraken If you have a wall to hide behind it's not too bad. If you get caught out in the open water you are in serious trouble. A scroll of fog or another source of clouds can break the kraken's LoS. Both the kraken and the tentacles are cold-blooded, so they can be slowed by a freezing weapon.
!learn mv kraken[2] kraken[3]
!learn mv kraken[1] kraken[4]

!learn add brogue[3] Early game strategy: Loot the first 4 floors, don't ID anything. Throw darts at conjurers/bats or run from them. Regen and do the floor 3 lock-and-key puzzle (if you need lev it's in your inventory). Now blind quaff for detect magic. From now on, throw 'red' potions at enemies to id them instead of quaffing them. Focus all enchants on the first worthy item. Use 'D' before 
!learn add brogue[3] Early game strategy: Loot the first 4 floors, don't ID anything. Throw darts at conjurers/bats or run from them. Regen and do the floor 3 lock-and-key puzzle (if you need lev it's in your inventory). Now blind quaff for detect magic. From now on, throw 'red' potions at enemies to id them instead of quaffing them. Enchant the first useful item. Use 'D' before further use-iding.
!learn add brogue[3] Early game strategy: Loot the first 4 floors, don't ID anything. Throw darts at conjurers/bats or run. At full hp, do the D:3 lock-and-key puzzle (if it needs lev you have it already). Blind quaff for detect magic. Enchant your puzzle loot. Throw 'red' potions at nasties to ID. Use 'D' as a reference.
!learn add brogue[4] Survival tips: Use your darts, they're guaranteed for a reason. When you see a monkey, wield/drop your darts so they can't be stolen. Drop your weapon/armour, melee acid blobs naked. Mouse over things to find out if you'll die next turn, entries in the sidebar to light where they are. All gasses, foilage and bridges can be ignited.
!learn add brogue[5] Survival tips: Normal melee attacks can't be done diagonally around corners (but axe attacks/projectiles work). Fight spiders alone. When low on hp, search a few times in every new room (searches do LOS). Fight jellies with them in the room and you on the doorway, and prioritize ones that appear behind you.
!learn add brogue[6] Survival tips: You are stealthier when immobile. Your dagger is weak, get a better weapon. Have an escape route/pillar dance circuit when you see something difficult. Monsters pursue aggressively up stairs. You get XP no matter how enemies die - be creative. Let sleeping OOD monsters lie - beware of allies waking them foolishly.
!learn edit brogue[3] s/Enchant your puzzle loot/Enchant your best item
!learn edit brogue[4] s/All/ALL
!learn edit brogue[5] s/$/ Alternatively, jellies cannot swim.
!learn add brogue[7] Survival tips: While you can push past allies, enemies cannot push past each other - trap conjurers behind their blades, et cetera. Taking a swim is a good way to avoid some enemies - all your items will wash onto shore. (Also, watch out for eels.)

It took more XP to raise the Spellcasting skill than a normal skill at the same aptitude, and less XP to raise Stealth, Evocations and Invocations. !learn add badforum Advanced Alchemy- Each potion has a Concentration rating from 1-5. A potion that is 3/5 is less pure than a 5/5 potion, which makes it less effective. This allows the ability to mix potions in different ways. For example- A 3/5 Potion of Confusion combined with a 2/5 Potion of Magic Nets the player a Potion of Amnesia, but a 3/5 Potion of Magic mixed with a 2/5 Potion of Confusion nets the player a Potion of Transmutation
